[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDuring an OSS-Fuzz run of the libxml2 “api” fuzz target, AddressSanitizer detected [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39ma double-free in the function `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfile `fuzz/api.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. A block[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof memory allocated via `xmlFuzzMalloc`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`xmlStrdup` and used to create a comment [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnode is freed twice, causing the process to abort.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m• Issue overview  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  While executing the “api” fuzz harness with a specially crafted input, the fuzzer[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minvoked `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput`. AddressSanitizer reported that the same [0m[1;36m11[0m[39m-byte [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mregion was freed twice in the same thread, triggering an abort.[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m• Vulnerability type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  This is a double-free vulnerability. Double-free can lead to memory corruption, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcrashes, or potential code execution if exploited.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m• Key observations  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  – The initial allocation happens at:  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    • `malloc` in `asan_malloc_linux.cpp`  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    • `xmlFuzzMalloc` in `fuzz/fuzz.[0m[1;92mc:127[0m[39m`  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    • `xmlStrndup` in `xmlstring.[0m[1;92mc:57[0m[39m` → `xmlNewComment` in `tree.[0m[1;92mc:2583[0m[39m` → first [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfree in `fuzz/api.[0m[1;92mc:1339[0m[39m`.  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  – The second free of the same address is invoked later in `fuzz/api.[0m[1;92mc:3580[0m[39m`.  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  – AddressSanitizer marks the scariness level as [0m[1;36m42[0m[39m and aborts execution.  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  – The crash reproduces reliably with the provided testcase under `-[0m[33mruns[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m100[0m[39m`.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m• Code areas for investigation  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. **fuzz/api.c** around lines [0m[1;36m1339[0m[39m and [0m[1;36m3580[0m[39m: examine how comment nodes are [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcreated, tracked, and freed in the harness.  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. **tree.c** [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`xmlNewComment`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: review ownership and lifecycle of the string [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpassed to the new comment node.  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. **xmlstring.c** [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`xmlStrdup`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`xmlStrndup`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: verify allocation semantics.  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. **fuzz/fuzz.c** [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`xmlFuzzMalloc`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: check whether the fuzz allocation wrapper [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maligns with the library’s free logic.  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Overall memory management in the comment-node code paths to ensure each [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocation is freed exactly once.[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The duplicate `[0m[1;35mfree[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` calls happen in the fuzzer’s test callback, not in the [0m    [2m                [0m
